<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Generation_II"><a href="/wiki/Generation_II" title="Generation II">Generation II</a></span></h3>
<table align="center" style="border-radius: 10px; -moz-border-radius: 10px; -webkit-border-radius: 10px; -khtml-border-radius: 10px; -icab-border-radius: 10px; -o-border-radius: 10px;; border: 2px solid #DAA520; background: #DAA520;">
<tr>
<th style="border-top-left-radius: 5px; -moz-border-radius-topleft: 5px; -webkit-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -khtml-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -icab-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -o-border-top-left-radius: 5px; background: #D6D6D6"> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pok%C3%A9mon_by_Johto_Pok%C3%A9dex_number" title="List of Pokémon by Johto Pokédex number"><span style="color:#000;">Jdex</span></a>
</th>
<th style="background: #D6D6D6"> Ndex
</th>
<th style="background: #D6D6D6"> MS
</th>
<th style="background: #D6D6D6"> Pokémon
</th>
<th style="border-top-right-radius: 5px; -moz-border-radius-topright: 5px; -webkit-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -khtml-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -icab-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -o-border-top-right-radius: 5px; background: #D6D6D6" colspan="2"> Type
</th></tr>
<tr style="background:#FFFFFF;">
<td style="font-family:Monospace;"> #001
</td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Generation_IV"><a href="/wiki/Generation_IV" title="Generation IV">Generation IV</a></span></h3>
<table align="center" style="border-radius: 10px; -moz-border-radius: 10px; -webkit-border-radius: 10px; -khtml-border-radius: 10px; -icab-border-radius: 10px; -o-border-radius: 10px;; border: 2px solid #AAAAFF; background: #AAAAFF;">
<tr>
<th style="border-top-left-radius: 5px; -moz-border-radius-topleft: 5px; -webkit-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -khtml-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -icab-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -o-border-top-left-radius: 5px; background: #FFC8C8"> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pok%C3%A9mon_by_Sinnoh_Pok%C3%A9dex_number" title="List of Pokémon by Sinnoh Pokédex number"><span style="color:#000;">Sdex</span></a>
</th>
<th style="background: #FFC8C8"> Ndex
</th>
<th style="background: #FFC8C8"> MS
</th>
<th style="background: #FFC8C8"> Pokémon
</th>
<th style="border-top-right-radius: 5px; -moz-border-radius-topright: 5px; -webkit-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -khtml-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -icab-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -o-border-top-right-radius: 5px; background: #FFC8C8" colspan="2"> Type
</th></tr>
<tr style="background:#FFFFFF;">
<td style="font-family:Monospace;"> #001
</td>
<td style="font-family:Monospace;"> #387
</td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Generation_V"><a href="/wiki/Generation_V" title="Generation V">Generation V</a></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Generation_VII">Generation VII</span></h3>
<table align="center" style="border-radius: 10px; -moz-border-radius: 10px; -webkit-border-radius: 10px; -khtml-border-radius: 10px; -icab-border-radius: 10px; -o-border-radius: 10px;; border: 2px solid #F1912B; background: #F1912B;">
<tr>
<th style="border-top-left-radius: 5px; -moz-border-radius-topleft: 5px; -webkit-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -khtml-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -icab-border-top-left-radius: 5px; -o-border-top-left-radius: 5px; background: #90BDDC"> Adex

<th style="border-top-right-radius: 5px; -moz-border-radius-topright: 5px; -webkit-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -khtml-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -icab-border-top-right-radius: 5px; -o-border-top-right-radius: 5px; background: #90BDDC" colspan="2"> Type

<tr style="background:#FFFFFF;">
<td style="font-family:Monospace;"> #???

<td style="font-family:Monospace;"> #???
</td>
